Reporting and enforcement
=========================

Learn about reporting content on YouTube, the actions our teams take when reviewing content, and what this means for you.

Reporting
---------

*   [Report inappropriate content](/youtube/answer/2802027?hl=en&ref_topic=9387085)

*   [Report policy-violative ads](/youtube/answer/10684207?hl=en&ref_topic=9387085)

*   [Your content & Restricted Mode](/youtube/answer/7354993?hl=en&ref_topic=9387083)

*   [View your Reporting History](/youtube/answer/7687979?hl=en&ref_topic=9387083)
